\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename Derived$>$\newline
class Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base$<$ Derived $>$}
\doxylink{classEigen_1_1CwiseBinaryOpImpl}{Base} class of any sparse matrices or sparse expressions. 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Derived} & is the derived type, e.\+g. a sparse matrix type, or an expression, etc.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
This class can be extended with the help of the plugin mechanism described on the page Topic\+Customizing\+\_\+\+Plugins by defining the preprocessor symbol {\ttfamily EIGEN\+\_\+\+SPARSEMATRIXBASE\+\_\+\+PLUGIN}. 

\label{doc-typedef-members}
\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_doc-typedef-members}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1Matrix}{Matrix}}$<$Scalar,\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_af5971b1d24ac9039b0b9436d5d87d485a456cda7b9d938e57194036a41d634604}{Rows\+At\+Compile\+Time}},\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_af5971b1d24ac9039b0b9436d5d87d485a27ba349f075d026c1f51d1ec69aa5b14}{Cols\+At\+Compile\+Time}}$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Dense\+Matrix\+Type}

type of the equivalent dense matrix \Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_aaec8ace6efb785c81d442931c3248d88}\index{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$}!RealScalar@{RealScalar}}
\index{RealScalar@{RealScalar}!Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RealScalar}{RealScalar}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_aaec8ace6efb785c81d442931c3248d88} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1NumTraits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$Scalar$>$\+::\+Real \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Real\+Scalar}

This is the "{}real scalar"{} type; if the {\itshape Scalar} type is already real numbers (e.\+g. int, float or double) then {\itshape \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_aaec8ace6efb785c81d442931c3248d88}{Real\+Scalar}} is just the same as {\itshape Scalar}. If {\itshape Scalar} is {\itshape std\+::complex$<$\+T$>$} then \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_aaec8ace6efb785c81d442931c3248d88}{Real\+Scalar} is {\itshape T}.

Is\+Vector\+At\+Compile\+Time&This is set to true if either the number of rows or the number of columns is known at compile-\/time to be equal to 1. Indeed, in that case, we are dealing with a column-\/vector (if there is only one column) or with a row-\/vector (if there is only one row). \\

a fixed-\/size expression of a block of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.

The template parameters {\itshape NRows} and {\itshape NCols} are the number of rows and columns in the block.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{block()}{block()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a350f08d56eb9ea6e62a55079bd9e9fa6} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$int NRows, int NCols$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_1_1FixedBlockXpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ NRows, NCols $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{start\+Row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{start\+Col}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{block\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{block\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a block of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em NRows} & number of rows in block as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em NCols} & number of columns in block as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start\+Row} & the first row in the block \\
\hline
{\em start\+Col} & the first column in the block \\
\hline
{\em block\+Rows} & number of rows in block as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em block\+Cols} & number of columns in block as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for blocks where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape block\+Rows} should equal {\itshape NRows} unless {\itshape NRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The usage of of this overload is discouraged from Eigen 3.\+4, better used the generic \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a9497c0f6429643b6088dfc5e06a2bcf7}{block(\+Index,\+Index,\+NRows\+Type,\+NCols\+Type)}, here is the one-\/to-\/one complete equivalence\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{mat.template\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a9497c0f6429643b6088dfc5e06a2bcf7}{block<NRows,NCols>}}(i,j,\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a1944e9fa9ce7937bfc3a87b2cb94371f}{rows}},\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_aca7ce296424ef6e478ab0fb19547a7ee}{cols}})\ \ \ \ \ <-\/-\/>\ \ mat.block(i,j,fix<NRows>(\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a1944e9fa9ce7937bfc3a87b2cb94371f}{rows}}),fix<NCols>(\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_aca7ce296424ef6e478ab0fb19547a7ee}{cols}}))}

\end{DoxyCode}
 If we known that, e.\+g., NRows==Dynamic and NCols!=Dynamic, then the equivalence becomes\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{mat.template\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a9497c0f6429643b6088dfc5e06a2bcf7}{block<Dynamic,NCols>}}(i,j,\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a1944e9fa9ce7937bfc3a87b2cb94371f}{rows}},NCols)\ \ <-\/-\/>\ \ mat.block(i,j,\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a1944e9fa9ce7937bfc3a87b2cb94371f}{rows}},fix<NCols>)}

\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename NRows\+Type, typename NCols\+Type$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_1_1FixedBlockXpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1get__fixed__value}{internal\+::get\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+value}}$<$ NRows\+Type $>$\+::value, \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1get__fixed__value}{internal\+::get\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+value}}$<$ NCols\+Type $>$\+::value $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{start\+Row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{start\+Col}{, }\item[{NRows\+Type}]{block\+Rows}{, }\item[{NCols\+Type}]{block\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a block in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with either dynamic or fixed sizes.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start\+Row} & the first row in the block \\
\hline
{\em start\+Col} & the first column in the block \\
\hline
{\em block\+Rows} & number of rows in the block, specified at either run-\/time or compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em block\+Cols} & number of columns in the block, specified at either run-\/time or compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em NRows\+Type} & the type of the value handling the number of rows in the block, typically \doxylink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}. \\
\hline
{\em NCols\+Type} & the type of the value handling the number of columns in the block, typically \doxylink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
Example using runtime (aka dynamic) sizes\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\textbackslash{}newin\{3.\+4\}\+:

The number of rows {\itshape block\+Rows} and columns {\itshape block\+Cols} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. In the later case, {\ttfamily n} plays the role of a runtime fallback value in case {\ttfamily N} equals \doxylink{namespaceEigen_ad81fa7195215a0ce30017dfac309f0b2}{Eigen\+::\+Dynamic}. Here is an example with a fixed number of rows {\ttfamily NRows} and dynamic number of columns {\ttfamily cols\+:} 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{mat.block(i,j,fix<NRows>,\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_aca7ce296424ef6e478ab0fb19547a7ee}{cols}})}

\end{DoxyCode}


This function thus fully covers the features offered by the following overloads \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a3a98e606906dc31ef19e27a3b2ef2d12}{block$<$\+NRows,\+NCols$>$(\+Index, Index)}, and \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a350f08d56eb9ea6e62a55079bd9e9fa6}{block$<$\+NRows,\+NCols$>$(\+Index, Index, Index, Index)} that are thus obsolete. Indeed, this generic version avoids redundancy, it preserves the argument order, and prevents the need to rely on the template keyword in templated code.

but with less redundancy and more consistency as it does not modify the argument order and seamlessly enable hybrid fixed/dynamic sizes.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Even in the case that the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size matrix, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
class \doxylink{classEigen_1_1Block}{Block}, fix, fix$<$\+N$>$(int) 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_1_1FixedBlockXpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::bottom\+Left\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a bottom-\/left corner of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

{\em NRows\+Type} & the type of the value handling the number of rows in the block, typically \doxylink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}.\\

\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


The number of rows {\itshape n} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. See \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a9497c0f6429643b6088dfc5e06a2bcf7}{block() } for the details. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of the coefficient-\/wise == operator of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this and {\itshape other} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
this performs an exact comparison, which is generally a bad idea with floating-\/point types. In order to check for equality between two vectors or matrices with floating-\/point coefficients, it is generally a far better idea to use a fuzzy comparison as provided by is\+Approx() and is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than().
\end{DoxyWarning}

\index{cwiseNotEqual@{cwiseNotEqual}!Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cwiseNotEqual()}{cwiseNotEqual()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a1d2182afda06d0a1b244c31a1ebd7d92} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1CwiseBinaryOp}{Cwise\+Binary\+Op}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1numext_1_1not__equal__to}{numext\+::not\+\_\+equal\+\_\+to}}$<$ Scalar $>$, const Derived, const Other\+Derived $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::cwise\+Not\+Equal (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const EIGEN\+\_\+\+CURRENT\+\_\+\+STORAGE\+\_\+\+BASE\+\_\+\+CLASS$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of the coefficient-\/wise != operator of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this and {\itshape other} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
this performs an exact comparison, which is generally a bad idea with floating-\/point types. In order to check for equality between two vectors or matrices with floating-\/point coefficients, it is generally a far better idea to use a fuzzy comparison as provided by is\+Approx() and is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than().
\end{DoxyWarning}

The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape n} should equal {\itshape N} unless {\itshape N} is {\itshape Dynamic}.

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename NType$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_1_1FixedSegmentReturnType}{Fixed\+Segment\+Return\+Type}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1get__fixed__value}{internal\+::get\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+value}}$<$ NType $>$\+::value $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::head (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{NType}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of the first coefficients of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with either dynamic or fixed sizes.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em n} & the number of coefficients in the segment \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em NType} & the type of the value handling the number of coefficients in the segment, typically \doxylink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


The number of coefficients {\itshape n} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. See \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a9497c0f6429643b6088dfc5e06a2bcf7}{block() } for the details.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Even in the case that the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a9d4d71b3f34389e6fc01f2b86e43f7a4}\index{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$}!operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}@{operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}}
\index{operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}@{operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}!Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}()}{operator*()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a9d4d71b3f34389e6fc01f2b86e43f7a4} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1Product}{Product}}$<$ Derived, Other\+Derived, Alias\+Free\+Product $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::operator\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of the product of two sparse matrices. By default a conservative product preserving the symbolic non zeros is performed. The automatic pruning of the small values can be achieved by calling the \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned()} function in which case a totally different product algorithm is employed\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{C\ =\ (A*B).\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}();\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ suppress\ numerical\ zeros\ (exact)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{C\ =\ (A*B).\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}(ref);}
\DoxyCodeLine{C\ =\ (A*B).\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}(ref,epsilon);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily ref} is a meaningful non zero reference value. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with values smaller than {\itshape reference} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} {\itshape epsilon} removed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This method is typically used in conjunction with the product of two sparse matrices to automatically prune the smallest values as follows\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{C\ =\ (A*B).\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}();\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ suppress\ numerical\ zeros\ (exact)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{C\ =\ (A*B).\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_ac8d0414b56d9d620ce9a698c1b281e5d}{pruned}}(ref,epsilon);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily ref} is a meaningful non zero reference value. \Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a47a21ed23d5d10618ac0aca93903a32e}\index{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrixBase$<$ Derived $>$}!real@{real}}

an expression of a segment (i.\+e. a vector block) in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with either dynamic or fixed sizes.

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


The number of coefficients {\itshape n} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. See \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a9497c0f6429643b6088dfc5e06a2bcf7}{block() } for the details.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Even in the case that the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape n} should equal {\itshape N} unless {\itshape N} is {\itshape Dynamic}.

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename NType$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_1_1FixedSegmentReturnType}{Fixed\+Segment\+Return\+Type}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1get__fixed__value}{internal\+::get\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+value}}$<$ NType $>$\+::value $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::tail (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{NType}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a last coefficients of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with either dynamic or fixed sizes.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em n} & the number of coefficients in the segment \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em NType} & the type of the value handling the number of coefficients in the segment, typically \doxylink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


The number of coefficients {\itshape n} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. See \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a9497c0f6429643b6088dfc5e06a2bcf7}{block() } for the details.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Even in the case that the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$int CRows, int CCols$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_1_1FixedBlockXpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::top\+Left\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a top-\/left corner of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.
